<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*somъ</i>.

</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li>to close
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сомкнуть.html>сомкну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>somknútʹ</b> glaza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to close one's eyes</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ние</a> (1309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">somnénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>doubt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́нии</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>somnénii</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">doubt about</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ния</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez <b>somnénija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">without doubt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>question

***сон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сон</a> (475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъ̀nъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*supnós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">son</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сна</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>снов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sleep</li>
<li>dream (imaginary events seen in the mind while sleeping)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1916—1922</b>,  Александр <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>Грин</a> (Alexander Grin),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:алый.html>А́лые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>паруса</a></cite>  | <cite>Scarlet sails</cite> | , filmed in 1961:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">далеко́-далеко́ <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:увидеть.html>уви́дел</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сне́</a></b></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dalekó-dalekó otsjúda ja uvídel tebjá vo <b>sné</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Far, far away I saw you in my <b>dream</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***сонм.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сонм.html>сонм</a> (26466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">съньмъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭnĭmŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъ(n)ьmъ</i>. Identical to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">съём</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sʺjom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сойм</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sojm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совать.html>суём</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sujóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сейм</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sejm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сонм.html>сонм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sonm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сонм.html>со́нма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сонм.html>со́нмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сонм.html>со́нмов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>host, crowd</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soobrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соображать.html>сообража́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soobražátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to consider, to ponder (over), to think (over / out); to weigh, to weigh the pros and the cons</li>
<li>to understand, to grasp, to guess, to figure out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prepare (food), to cook
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорый.html>ско́рую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Máma na skóruju rúku <b>soobrazíla</b> obéd.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Mum quickly prepared lunch.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́ть</a>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soobrazívšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́ть</a> (1961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soobrazítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соображать.html>сообража́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to consider, to ponder (over), to think (over / out); to weigh, to weigh the pros and the cons</li>
<li>to understand, to grasp, to guess, to figure out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prepare (food), to cook, to whip up, to fix
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорый.html>ско́рую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Máma na skóruju rúku <b>soobrazíla</b> obéd.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Mum, quick-handed, whipped up a little something for dinner.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink alcohol
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сообразить.html>сообрази́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>трои́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soobrazítʹ</b> na troíx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have/organise a drink (alcohol) in a group of three</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщать.html>сообща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soobščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщаться.html>сообща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soobščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сообщи́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be reported
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщаться.html>сообща́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>soobščájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">as is reported; according to reports; it is reported that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщаться.html>сообща́ется</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:захваченный.html>захва́чено</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заложник.html>зало́жников</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>soobščájetsja</b>, zaxváčeno désjatʹ zalóžnikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten persons are reported to have been taken hostage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be communicated, to communicate</li>
<li>to be in communication <i>(with)</i>, to communicate <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to be imparted <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщать.html>сообща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soobščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ща́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ться</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщение.html>сообще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soobščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщение.html>сообще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщение.html>сообще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщение.html>сообще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>report, communication, message
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обрадоваться.html>обра́довалась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твоему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщение.html>сообще́нию</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja óčenʹ obrádovalasʹ tvojemú <b>soobščéniju</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I was very happy about your <b>message</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>statement, announcement, information</li></ol>

***сообщить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сообщить.html>сообщи́ть</a> (599)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщить.html>сообщи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soobščítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сообщать.html>сообща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to communicate, to report, to let know</li>
<li>to impart</li></ol>
